SELECT
	t.*,
	COUNT(1) OVER() AS visible_rows
FROM
(
	SELECT
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY id DESC) AS rn,
		id,
		current_state,
		filesize,
		report_content,
   		TO_CHAR(d_req, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_req,
   		TO_CHAR(d_last, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_last,
   		id_report,
   		canceled,
   		s_name
	FROM
		t_report_req
	WHERE
		is_enabled = 1 AND
		is_mail = 0 AND
		id_user = :id_user/* AND
		downloaded = 0*/
) t
WHERE
	(:id_req > 0 AND :id_req = t.id) OR
	t.rn BETWEEN :start_num_row AND :last_num_row
bound id_user as INT 21=1 bound start_num_row as INT 21=1 bound last_num_row as INT 21=10 bound id_req as INT 21=0

SELECT
    id,
    parent_id,
    indicator_id,
    name,
    level,
    description,
    DISPLAY_BY_DEFAULT,
    IS_PERIOD,
    IS_BUDGET_YEAR,
    IS_PLAN_PERIOD,
    IS_PLAN_YEAR,
    IS_PERIOD_SEND_REQUEST,
    IS_PERIOD_SEND_CONCLUS,
    ORD
FROM
(
    SELECT
        bh.block_id AS id,
        b.parent_id,
        b.indicator_id,
        b.name,
        i.description_br AS description,
        bh.DISPLAY_BY_DEFAULT,
        b.IS_PERIOD,
        b.IS_BUDGET_YEAR,
        b.IS_PLAN_PERIOD,
        b.IS_PLAN_YEAR,
        b.IS_PERIOD_SEND_REQUEST,
        b.IS_PERIOD_SEND_CONCLUS,
        bh.ORD
    FROM
        s_lnk_block_header bh
    INNER JOIN
        s_sp_block b
        ON
            b.id = bh.block_id
    LEFT JOIN
        f_sp_indicators i
        ON
            i.entity_id = b.indicator_id and TO_DATE (SYS_CONTEXT ('eaist_context', 'version_date'),'DD.MM.YYYY') between DATE_START and DATE_END 
    WHERE
        bh.header_id IN
        (
            SELECT
                h.id
            FROM
                s_sp_reports r
            INNER JOIN
                s_sp_header h
                ON
                    h.report_id = r.id
            WHERE
                r.id = :REPORT_ID
        )
    ORDER BY
        bh.ORD
)
CONNECT BY
    PRIOR id = parent_id
START WITH
    parent_id IS NULL
    ORDER SIBLINGS BY ORD
bound REPORT_ID as INT 21=32

16data_inp 0.001:
SELECT
	t.*,
	COUNT(1) OVER() AS visible_rows
FROM
(
	SELECT
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY id DESC) AS rn,
		id,
		current_state,
		filesize,
		report_content,
   		TO_CHAR(d_req, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_req,
   		TO_CHAR(d_last, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_last,
   		id_report,
   		canceled,
   		s_name
	FROM
		t_report_req
	WHERE
		is_enabled = 1 AND
		is_mail = 0 AND
		id_user = :id_user/* AND
		downloaded = 0*/
) t
WHERE
	(:id_req > 0 AND :id_req = t.id) OR
	t.rn BETWEEN :start_num_row AND :last_num_row
bound id_user as INT 21=1 bound start_num_row as INT 21=1 bound last_num_row as INT 21=10 bound id_req as INT 21=0

            ENABLED, SUBTITLE, MODULE,
             R,
             W
          FROM MSK_EAIST_ANALYTIC.rep_core_menu RCM
          LEFT JOIN (
            SELECT MENU_ID m_id, MIN(R) AS R, MIN(
              CASE WHEN R > 0 THEN W ELSE 0 END
            ) AS W
            FROM CORE_ADMIN_MSK. V_USER_PRIVS VUP

              VUP.SYS_ID=777 AND NOT MENU_ID IS NULL
            GROUP BY MENU_ID
          ) S ON RCM.MENU_ID||'' = S.M_ID||''
           WHERE R > 0 AND ENABLED=1 
          ORDER BY N_ORDER, NAME

SELECT
					m.name,
					m.show,
					m.menu_id,
					m.subtitle,
					m.ext,
					m.class_name
				FROM
					rep_core_menu m
				WHERE
					m.enabled = 1 AND
					m.hidden <> 1 AND
					m.parent_id = :par_id AND
					EXISTS
					(
						SELECT
							1
						FROM
							MSK_EAIST_ANALITYC_DATA.REF_REPORTS_SOURCES ref
						WHERE
							ref.id_report = m.menu_id AND
							ref.is_enable = 1
					)

SELECT
	*
FROM
(
	SELECT
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY id DESC) AS rn,
		id,
		current_state,
		filesize,
		report_content,
		TO_CHAR(d_req, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_req,
		TO_CHAR(d_last, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_last,
		id_report,
		downloaded,
		canceled,
		s_name
	FROM
		T_REPORT_REQ
	WHERE
		is_enabled = 1 AND
		is_mail = 0 AND
		id_user = :id_user
)
WHERE
	rn BETWEEN :start_num_row AND :last_num_row
bound id_user as INT 21=1 bound start_num_row as INT 21=1 bound last_num_row as INT 21=10
